ResourceAll {\n    32→\t\t\treturn true\n    33→\t\t}\n    34→\t\t// if we have an exact match, we match\n    35→\t\tif ruleResource == combinedRequestedResource {\n    36→\t\t\treturn true\n    37→\t\t}\n    38→\n    39→\t\t// We can also match a */subresource.\n    40→\t\t// if there isn't a subresource, then continue\n    41→\t\tif len(requestedSubresource) == 0 {\n    42→\t\t\tcontinue\n 189→\t\tif len(r.PolicyRule.ResourceNames) != 0 {\n   190→\t\t\tillegalVerbs := []string{}\n   191→\t\t\tfor _, verb := range r.PolicyRule.Verbs {\n   192→\t\t\t\tswitch verb {\n   193→\t\t\t\tcase rule.Resources matching.\nfunc ResourceMatches(rule *PolicyRule, combinedRequestedResource, requestedSubresource string) bool {\n\tfor _, ruleResource := range rule.Resources {\n\t\t// if everything is allowed, we match\n\t\tif ruleResource == ResourceAll {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\t// if we have an exact match, we match\n\t\tif ruleResource == combinedRequestedResource {\n\t\t\treturn in the format */subresource, then we don't match, continue\n\t\tif len(ruleResource) == len(requestedSubresource)+2 &&\n\t\t\tstrings.HasPrefix(ruleResource, \"*/\") 26→func VerbMatches(rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, requestedVerb string) bool {\n    27→\tfor _, ruleVerb := range rule.Verbs {\n    28→\t\tif ruleVerb == rbacv1.VerbAll {\n    29→\t\t\treturn true\n rbacv1.ResourceAll {\n    56→\t\t\treturn true\n    57→\t\t}\n    58→\t\t// if we have an exact match, we match\n    59→\t\tif ruleResource == combinedRequestedResource {\n    60→\t\t\treturn true\n    61→\t\t}\n    62→\n    63→\t\t// We can also match a */subresource.\n    64→\t\t// if there isn't a subresource, then continue\n    65→\t\tif len(requestedSubresource) == 0 {\n    66→\t\t\tcontinue\n    67→\t\t}\n    68→\t\t// if the rule isn't in the format */subresource, then we don't match, continue\n    69→\t\tif len(ruleResource) == len(requestedSubresource)+2 &&\n    70→\t\t\tstrings.HasPrefix(ruleResource, \"*/\") &&\n    71→\t\t\tstrings.HasSuffix(ruleResource, requestedSubresource) {\n    72→\t\t\treturn true\n    73→\n    74→\t\t}\n    75→\t}\n    76→\n    77→\treturn false\n    78→}\n    79→\n    80→func ResourceNameMatches(rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, requestedName string) bool {\n    81→\tif len(rule.ResourceNames) == 0 {\n    82→\t\treturn true\n    83→\t}\n    84→\n    85→\tfor _, ruleName := range rule.ResourceNames {\n    86→\t\tif ruleName == requestedName {\n    87→\t\t\treturn true\n    88→\t\t}\n    89→\t}\n    90→\n    91→\treturn false\n    92→}\n    93→\n    94→func NonResourceURLMatches(rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, requestedURL string) bool {\n    95→\tfor _, ruleURL := range rule.NonResourceURLs {\n    96→\t\tif ruleURL ==
